тАЬnyAsa: pancAngasamyuta:тАЭ, тАЬanenaiva tu mantreNaтАЭ ityAdikaLAlE bharanyAsamE angi ennumiDam siddham. Let us see the first pramANa in full: рдирд┐рдХреНрд╖реЗрдкрд╛рдкрд░рдкрд░реНрдпрд╛рдпреЛ рдиреНрдпрд╛рд╕рдГ рдкрдЮреНрдЪрд╛рдЩреНрдЧрд╕рдВрдпреБрддрдГред рд╕рдВрдиреНрдпрд╛рд╕рд╕реНрддреНрдпрд╛рдЧ рдЗрддреНрдпреБрдЦреНрдирдГ рд╢рд░рдгрд╛рдЧрддрд┐рд░рд┐рддреНрдпрдкрд┐рее nikshepAparaparyAyo nyAsa: pancAngasamyuta: | samnyAsastyAga ityukta: SaraNAgatirityapi || - -LakshmI tantram, 17-75 Meaning: nyAsam, which is synonymous with nikshepa, has five components. It is also referred to as sanyAsa, tyAga or SaraNAgati. This confirms the fact that surrender is the main means which has five

132

components, as we discussed earlier. Now, the next pramANam quoted by SwAmi DeSikan: рдЕрдиреЗрдиреИрд╡ рддреБ рдордиреНрддреНрд░реЗрдг рд╕реНрд╡рд╛рддреНрдорд╛рдирдВ рдордпрд┐ рдирд┐рдХреНрд╖рд┐рдкреЗрддреНред рдордпрд┐ рдирд┐рдХреНрд╖рд┐рдкреНрддрдХрд░реНрддрд╡реНрдпрдГ рдХреГрддрдХреГрддреНрдпреЛ рднрд╡рд┐рд╖реНрдпрддрд┐рее anenaiva tu mantreNa svAtmAnam mayi nikshipet | mayi nikshipta-kartavya: krtakrtyo bhavishyati || –sAtyaki tantram Meaning:
With this mantram one should surrender oneтАЩs self to Me. The one, who has surrendered to Me the responsibility of doing what should be done, becomes one who has accomplished his duty.
Thus, the surrender of the responsibility of protection (bhara-samarpaNam) should be chiefly thought of while uttering the dvaya mantram of prapatti. SwAmi DeSikan concludes: рдЗрддреНрдпрд╛рджрд┐ роХро│ро╛ро▓рпЗ рднрд░рдиреНрдпрд╛рд╕ роорпЗ роЕроЩрпНроХро┐ роОройрпНройрпБрооро┐роЯроорпН рд╕рд┐рджреНрдз роорпН.
ityAdikaLAlE bharanyAsamE angi ennumiDam siddham.
From the above and other such pramANams it is clear that the surrendering of the responsibility of protection to the Lord, that is, prapatti, is the principal means that has five components. SwAmi DeSikan proceeds with the questions on the components of prapatti: тАЬрдкреНрд░рдкрддреНрддрд┐рдВ рддрд╛рдВ рдкреНрд░рдпреБрдЮреНрдЬреАрдд рд╕реНрд╡рд╛рдЩреНрдЧреИрдГ рдкрдЮреНрдЪрднрд┐рд░рд╛рд╡реГрддрд╛рдВтАЭ

тАЬprapattim tAm prayunjIta svAngai: pancabhirAvrtAmтАЭ enRu angamAna AnukUlya sankalpAtikaLai sambhAvita-svabhAvam enpArkku uttarakAlattil AnukUlyAdikaLuDaiya aniyamattilE tAtparyam.
SwAmi DeSikan refers to a pramANa in support of the five components of prapatti тАУ тАЬрдкреНрд░рдкрддреНрддрд┐рдВ рддрд╛рдВ рдкреНрд░рдпреБрдЮреНрдЬреАрдд рд╕реНрд╡рд╛рдЩреНрдЧреИрдГ рдкрдЮреНрдЪрднрд┐рд░рд╛рд╡реГрддрд╛рдВтАЭ, тАЬprapattim tAm prayunjIta svAngai: pancabhirAvrtAmтАЭ тАУ Let us see this in full: рдкреНрд░рдкрддреНрддрд┐рдВ рддрд╛рдВ рдкреНрд░рдпреБрдЮреНрдЬреАрдд рд╕реНрд╡рд╛рдЩреНрдЧреИрдГ рдкрдЮреНрдЪрднрд┐рд░рд╛рд╡реГрддрд╛рдВред рдкреНрд░рд╛рддрд┐рдХреВрд▓реНрдпрдВ рдкрд░рд┐рддреНрдпрдЦреНрдирдорд╛рдиреБрдХреВрд▓реНрдпрдВ рдЪ рд╕рдВрд╢реНрд░рд┐рддрдореНрее prapattim tAm prayunjIta svAngai: pancabhirAvrtAm | prAtikUlyam parityaktamAnukUlyam ca samSritam || (LakshmI tantram, 28-11) Meaning:
He (an aspirant for moksham) should perform prapatti in all its five components, with resolves such as, тАЬI give up all acts that would displease the Lord and thus be detrimental to attainment of moksham, and adopt only those would be conducive to moksham and hence please Him.тАЭ
In order to clarify, SwAmi DeSikan then refers to a view of some on the necessity of the presence of the components in the person who is to do prapatti. According to them, the components like AnukUlya sankalpam etc., are not necessary for prapatti and these would spontaneously be a part of one who intends to perform prapatti at the LordтАЩs feet. Their view is that there need be no hard and fast rule that these components be present in the person after the prapatti.

134

However, there is a rule that the prapanna can not live in whatever way he feels, points out SwAmi DeSikan: роЖроХрпИропро╛ро▓рпЗ, роорпЗро▓рпН рдЕрдкрд╛рдп-рд╕рдВрдкреНрд▓рд╡ родрпНродро┐ро▓рпБроорпН, рдЕрдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░-рд╡рд┐рд░реБрджреНрдз-рдЙрдкрд╛рдп-рдкрд░рд┐рдЧреНрд░рд╣ родрпНродро┐ро▓рпБроорпН рдкреБрдирдГ рдкреНрд░рдкрджрди роорпН рд╡рд┐рдзрд┐ роХрпНроХро┐ро▒родрпБ.
AkaiyAlE, mEl apAya-samplavattilum, adhikAri-viruddha-upAya-parigrahattilum puna: prapadanam vidhikkiRatu. If the components of prapatti are not compulsory, then some problems may arise. It may appear as though the prapanna is free to do as he pleases, and may even commit a sin! It is not so, as it has been laid down that after prapatti, if any sin is committed by the prapanna, he has to perform prapatti again. It is also laid down that if a prapanna adopts another means at variance to his state, he has to perform another prapatti in atonement. Hence, the prapanna can not act as he desires.
SwAmi DeSikan clears more doubts that would arise in the minds of people about the validity of the components of prapatti, like AnukUlya sankalpam, prAtikUlya varjanam etc.: роХрокрпЛрод-роиро╛ро│рпАроЬроЩрпНроХ-ро╡ро╛ройро░ро╛родро┐ ро╡рпНро░рпБродрпНродро╛роирпНродроЩрпНроХро│рпИрокрпН рокро╛ро░рпНродрпНродро╛ро▓рпН роЪро░рогро╛роХрод ройрпБроХрпНроХрпБродрпН родродрпНроХро╛ро▓родрпНродро┐ро▓рпБроорпН роЖроирпБроХрпВро▓рпНропро╛родро┐ роиро┐ропроорооро┐ройрпНро▒ро┐роХрпНроХрпЗ роЗро┐ро░рпБроХрпНроХ ро░роХрпНро╖ро┐роХрпНроХроХрпН роХрогрпНроЯрпЛроорпЗ роОройрпНройро┐ро▓рпН, ро▓рпЛроХродрпНродро┐ро▓рпН роХро╛ро░рпБрогро┐роХро░рпН рдзрд░реНрдо-рдЕрднрд┐рд╕рдиреНрдзрд┐ ро╡ро┐ро╢рпЗро╖родрпНродро╛ро▓рпЗ роЕрокрпНрокроЯро┐роХрпНроХрпБ ро░роХрпНро╖ро┐роХрпНроХро┐ро▒ро╛ро░рпН. роИро╢рпНро╡ро░ройрпН ро░роХрпНро╖ро┐роХрпНроХрпБроорпН рокрпЛродрпБ, родройрпНройрпБроЯрпИроп роиро┐ропрпЛроХродрпНродрпИ рдпрдерд╛рд╡рддреН роЕроирпБро╖рпНроЯро┐рокрпНрокро┐родрпНродрпБ ро░роХрпНро╖ро┐роХрпНроХрпБроорпН.
kapOda-nALIjanga-vAnarAdi vrttAntanglaip pArttAl caraNAgatanukkut tatkAlattilm AnukUlyAdi niyamaminRikkE irukka rakshikkak kaNDOmE ennil, lOkattil kAruNikar dharma-abhisandhi viSeshattAlE appaDikku rakshikkiRAr. ISvaran rakshikkum pOtu, tannuDaiya niyOkattai yathAvat anushTippittu rakshikkum.

135

A doubt arises as to whether one who undertakes to perform prapatti must observe the norm of doing only acts that please the Lord and give up acts that displease Him. But, this does not seem appropriate in the worldly context. The objection has reference to some stories that form part of the epics: роХрокрпЛрод-роиро╛ро│рпАроЬроЩрпНроХ-ро╡ро╛ройро░ро╛родро┐ ро╡рпНро░рпБродрпНродро╛роирпНродроЩрпНроХро│рпИрокрпН рокро╛ро░рпНродрпНродро╛ро▓рпН ,
kapOda-nALIjanga-vAnarAdi vruttAntangalaip pArttAl тАУ Looking at the stories of dove-hunter, crane-brahmin and monkey-hunterтАж. The first and the third stories were stated by Lord Raama in the YuddhakhANdam of ValmIki RaamaayaNa, while the second one is in the AraNya -parva of MahAbhAratam. The dove-hunter and the monkey-hunter stories are discussed by SwAmi DeSikan in detail in the abhaya-pradAna-sAram, another Chillarai rahasyam of his. The crane-brahmin story is a part of the story of dharma-vyAdar occurring in the MahAbhAratam. (For details please refer to the relevant sources.)
Referring to these stories, the critic says, тАЬIt is said that creatures like dove, crane and monkey saved the hunter, brAhmin and another hunter respectively though these creatures had borne the brunt of the acts of the latter. Hence, there is no need to insist on adopting acts pleasing to the Lord and giving up acts that do not please Him.тАЭ
SwAmi DeSikan replies to this objection as follows: тАЬ ро▓рпЛроХродрпНродро┐ро▓рпН роХро╛ро░рпБрогро┐роХро░рпН рдзрд░реНрдо-рдЕрднрд┐рд╕рдиреНрдзрд┐ ро╡ро┐ро╢рпЗро╖родрпНродро╛ро▓рпЗ роЕрокрпНрокроЯро┐роХрпНроХрпБ ро░роХрпНро╖ро┐роХрпНроХро┐ро▒ро╛ро░рпН. роИро╢рпНро╡ро░ройрпН ро░роХрпНро╖ро┐роХрпНроХрпБроорпН рокрпЛродрпБ, родройрпНройрпБроЯрпИроп роиро┐ропрпЛроХродрпНродрпИ рдпрдерд╛рд╡рддреН роЕроирпБро╖рпНроЯро┐рокрпНрокродрпБ ро░роХрпНро╖ро┐роХрпНроХрпБроорпН. тАЭ, тАЬlOkattil kAruNikar dharma-abhisandhi viSeshattAlE appaDikku rakshikkiRAr. ISvaran rakshikkum pOtu, tannuDaiya niyOkattai yathAvat anushTippittu rakshikkum.тАЭ

136

It is seen in the world that whenever anyone, who so ever he may be, is in a very difficult situation, a truly compassionate person extends a helping hand to the sufferer, as he thinks that it is his dharma. The same was the case with the dove, the crane and the monkey, which were naturally very compassionate and did not care as to whether the person in need was a friend or an enemy, as can be seen from the stories referred to earlier. They protected the hunter, the brAhmin and the hunter respectively considering it as an act of puNyam, even though they were harmed by the very same beings.
But, it is different in the case of the Lord. SwAmi DeSikan clarifies that though He is full of compassion, He will not extend protection disregarding the scriptural rules laid down by Himself. Hence, He will ensure that all the components of prapatti are followed by the prapanna. It is, therefore, essential to observe these angAs of prapatti, according to SwAmi DeSikan. SwAmi DeSikan further stresses the essentiality of the components of prapatti: роЗроЩрпНроХрпБ роЙродрпНродрооройрпН тАЬрдЕрд╣рдорд╕реНрдпрдкрд░рд╛рдзрд╛рдирд╛рдорд╛рд▓рдпреЛрд╜рдХрд┐рдЮреНрдЪрдиреЛрд╜рдЧрддрд┐рдГтАЩ, тАЬрдЕрдХрд┐рдЮреНрдЪрдиреЛрд╜рдирдиреНрдпрдЧрддрд┐рдГтАЭ
рдЗрддреНрдпрд╛рджрд┐ роХро│ро┐ро▒рпН роЪрпКройрпНрой рдЕрдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░ ро╡ро┐роЪрпЗро╖родрпНродрпЛроЯрпБроорпН роХро╛ро░рпНрокрогрпНропрооро╛роХро┐ро▒ роЕроЩрпНроХродрпНродрпЛроЯрпБроорпН роХрпВроЯро┐рой рднрд░ ро╕рооро░рпНрокрпНрокрогродрпНродро┐ро▓рпН роХро░рпНродрпНродро╛ро╡ро╛рой родройрпНройрпИроХрпН роХро╛роЯрпНроЯрпБроХро┐ро▒родрпБ.
ingu uttaman тАЬahamasyaparAdhAnAmAlayokincanogati:тАЭ, тАЬakincanonanyagati:тАЭ ityAdikaLiR sonna adhikAra-viSeshattODum kArpaNyamAiRa angattODum kUDina samarppaNattil karttAvAna tannaik kATTukiRatu. Now we shall consider this sentence of SwAmi DeSikan closely grammar based insights. He uses the term тАЬuttamanтАЭ to indicate the performer of prapatti. Grammatically it refers тАШthe first personтАЩ. The first part of the dvaya mantram ends as тАЬprapadyeтАЭ тАУ meaning (I) surrender. Here, the first person, тАЬIтАЭ is not specifically mentioned, but, the word тАЬprapadyeтАЭ terminates in the first person (singular), giving the meaning, тАЬI surrender.тАЭ In Sanskrit grammar, it is known

137

as тАЬuttama purusha eka vacanamтАЭ while in Tamil grammar, it is known as тАЬtanmai vikutiтАЭ. SwAmi DeSikan uses the term тАЬuttamanтАЭ to pack all these facts in a single word.

The Lord is compassionate but is never lenient to transgressors namperumAL - SrIrangam After this technical matter, we shall study the two quotes used by SwAmi DeSikan. The first one is from ahirbudhnya samhita - рдЕрд╣рдорд╕реНрдпрдкрд░рд╛рдзрд╛рдирд╛рдорд╛рд▓рдпреЛрд╜рдХрд┐рдЮреНрдЪрдиреЛрд╜рдЧрддрд┐рдГ ahamasyaparAdhAnAmAlayokincanogati: (ahirbudhnya samhita, 37-30) Meaning:
I am the abode of all transgressions; I have no means (upAyam) to save myself

138

and I have nothing else to attain other than You. The second quote is from a Slokam of SrI ALavantArтАЩs stotraratnam: рди рдзрд░реНрдордирд┐рд╖реНрдареЛрд╜рд╕реНрдорд┐ рди рдЪрд╛рддреНрдорд╡реЗрджреА
рди рднрдЦреНрдирд┐рдорд╛рдиреН рддреНрд╡рдЪреНрдЪрд░рдгрд╛рд░рд╡рд┐рдиреНрджреЗред рдЕрдХрд┐рдЮреНрдЪрдиреЛрд╜рдирдиреНрдпрдЧрддрд┐рдГ рд╢рд░рдгреНрдп
рддреНрд╡рддреНрдкрд╛рджрдореВрд▓рдВ рд╢рд░рдгрдВ рдкреНрд░рдкрджреНрдпреЗрее na dharmanishTho asmi na ca AtmavedI
na bhaktimAn tvat SaraNAravinde | akincana ananyagati: SaraNya
tvatpAdamUlam SarNam prapadye || (stotra ratnam-22) Meaning:
I have adopted neither the karma yogam nor the j~nAna yogam; nor have I done bhakti yogam towards the lotus feet of Yours. Oh the SaraNya (Saviour), I seek the refuge of Your lotus feet; I have no other means and nothing else to attain besides You. SwAmi Desikan continues further: тАЬрдЗрддреНрдпрд╛рджрд┐ роХро│ро┐ро▒рпН роЪрпКройрпНрой рдЕрдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░ -ро╡ро┐роЪрпЗро╖родрпНродрпЛроЯрпБроорпН роХро╛ро░рпНрокрогрпНропрооро╛роХро┐ро▒ роЕроЩрпНроХродрпНродрпЛроЯрпБроорпН роХрпВроЯро┐рой рднрд░ ро╕рооро░рпНрокрпНрокрогродрпНродро┐ро▓рпН роХро░рпНродрпНродро╛ро╡ро╛рой родройрпНройрпИроХрпН роХро╛роЯрпНроЯрпБроХро┐ро▒родрпБ. тАЭ, тАЬityAdikaLiR sonna adhikAra-viSeshattODum kArpaNyamAkiRa angattODum kUDina bhara samarppaNattil karttAvAna tannaik kATTukiRatu.тАЭ

139

Explanation:
By mentioning тАЬityAdikaLiR sonnaтАЭ, SwAmi DeSikan says, тАЬaccording to these and other pramANamsтАЭ, indicating there are more such references bearing the same message as stated in these two quotes. The crux of the sentence is:- The term тАЬprapadyeтАЭ indicates the performer of prapatti. He must have the qualifications as indicated in the above quotes. As already explained, the act of prapatti has six components, namely тАУ яВ╖яАаAnukUlya sankalpam тАУ the intention to do whatever is pleasing to the Lord; яВ╖яАаprAtikUlya varjanam тАУ the avoidance of whatever is displeasing to Him; яВ╖яАаmahA viSvAsam - absolute faith that He will grant protection; яВ╖яАаgoptrtva varaNam тАУ begging His protection and яВ╖яАаkArpaNyam тАУ the feeling of helplessness; besides the sixth one which is the main, that is,
яВ╖яАаAtmanikshepam тАУ the act of surrendering oneself.
For our convenience, we keep the order slightly changed as follows: яВ╖яАаAnukUlya sankalpam тАУ the resolve to do whatever is pleasing to the Lord; яВ╖яАаprAtikUlya varjanam тАУ the avoidance of whatever is displeasing to Him; яВ╖яАаkArpaNyam тАУ the feeling of helplessness; яВ╖яАаAtmanikshepam тАУ the act of surrendering oneself; яВ╖яАаgoptrtva varaNam тАУ begging His protection; and яВ╖яАаmahA viSvAsam - absolute faith that He will grant protection. The first qualification is, the prapanna should resolve that he will do only those

140

actions which are pleasing to the Lord. The second one is, he should totally give up doing acts which will displease Him. But, in practical life in this world, one comes under the influence or control of his own senses including the mind. There is every likely-hood of his committing mistakes, especially those beyond his control. It is natural. But, at the same time, immediately after the first mistake, a seeker of moksham realizes it and regrets for what he has done. This remorse leads to a sense of helplessness, which is the next qualification, known as kArpaNyam. This feeling of helplessness will make him realize that there are no means except surrendering himself at the feet of the Lord through an AcArya. This is the next component of prapatti, that is, Atmanikshepam. By doing so, he begs for protection from the Lord, which is the next component, goptrtva varaNam. After the prapatti, he should remain confident that the matter has been left in the hands of the Lord and He will take care of him. This faith is the most important and a vital component of prapatti, called, mahA viSvAsam, supreme faith. There after he should strictly adhere to the promises he had made at the time of prapatti. Now, coming back to the above sentence of SwAmi DeSikan: рдЕрдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░ -ро╡ро┐ро╢рпЗро╖родрпНродрпЛроЯрпБроорпН роХро╛ро░рпНрокрогрпНропрооро╛роХро┐ро▒ роЕроЩрпНроХродрпНродрпЛроЯрпБроорпН роХрпВроЯро┐рой
рднрд░ ро╕рооро░рпНрокрпНрокрогродрпНродро┐ро▓рпН роХро░рпНродрпНродро╛ро╡ро╛рой родройрпНройрпИроХрпН роХро╛роЯрпНроЯрпБроХро┐ро▒родрпБ. тАЭ,
adhikAra-viSeshattODum kArpaNyamAkiRa angattOdum kUDina bhara samarppaNattil karttAvAna tannaik kATTukiRatu.тАЭ
Here, by тАЬadhikAra-viSeshattODumтАЭ, SwAmi DeSikan refers to special qualifications, тАЬdoing actions that please the LordтАЭ and тАЬavoiding acts that would displease HimтАЭ. Along with these, he must have the sense of remorse for violations and a realization of total inability to adopt any other means or тАЬupAyamтАЭ, such as karma yogam, j~nAna yogam and bhakti yogam to cross of the ocean of samsAra in order to attain the Lord. The term, тАЬprapadyeтАЭ which ends in the singular first person, indicates the тАЬkartAтАЭ, the performer of prapatti who is endowed with the first two components combined with the third

141

component, тАЬkArpaNyamтАЭ, the feeling of total helplessness. SwAmi DeSikan now speaks about the attitude one should have while performing the prapatti: тАЬ роЕродрпБро╡рпБрооро╡ройродро┐ройрпНройро░рпБро│рпЗ тАЭ, тАЬ роЖро▒рпЖройроХрпНроХрпБ роиро┐ройрпН рокро╛родроорпЗ роЪро░рогро╛роХродрпН родроирпНродрпКро┤ро┐роирпНродро╛ропрпН тАЭ рдЗрддреНрдпрд╛рджрд┐ роХро│ро┐ро▒рпНрокроЯро┐ропрпЗ рокрпНро░рокродрпНродро┐ропрпБроорпН роЕро╡ройроЯро┐ропро╛роХ ро╡роирпНродродрпЖройрпНро▒рпБ рдЕрдиреБрд╕рдВрдзреЗрдп роорпН. тАЬatuvumavanatinnaruLEтАЭ, тАЬARenakku nin pAdamE caraNAkat tantozintAiтАЭ ityAdikaLiRpaDiyE prapattiyum avanaDiyAka vantatenRu anusandheyam.
SwAmi DeSikan says that a prapanna should keep in his mind that he is able to
perform prapatti only due to the LordтАЩs grace. He refers to two statements of SrI NammAzhvAr from his TiruvAimozhi, тАЬ роЕродрпБро╡рпБрооро╡ройродро┐ройрпНройро░рпБро│рпЗ тАЭ, тАЬ роЖро▒рпЖройроХрпНроХрпБ роиро┐ройрпН рокро╛родроорпЗ роЪро░рогро╛роХродрпН родроирпНродрпКро┤ро┐роирпНродро╛ропрпН тАЭ, тАЬatuvumavanatinnaruLEтАЭ, тАЬARenakku nin pAdamE caraNAkat tantozintAiтАЭ. Before studying the two quotes, we may recall an important practice followed by us, SrIvaishNavites, namely sAtvika tyAgam, while doing any duty. A person, who has developed wisdom due to the grace of an AcArya, will have no selfish attachment to the fruits of his actions. He will not think that he is doing the work on his own. This attitude is all the more necessary for a person seeking moksham. Even while he performs prapatti, he should keep in mind that he does so only due to the LordтАЩs grace and that the fruit also belongs to Him. This is what SrI NammAzhvAr says in the quotation above. Let us see his verse in full: роЙрогро░рпНро╡ро┐ро▓рпН роЙроорпНрокро░рпКро░рпБро╡ройрпИ роЕро╡ройродро░рпБро│ро╛ро▓рпН роЙро▒ро▒рпНрокрпКро░рпБроЯрпНроЯрпБ роОройрпН роЙрогро░рпНро╡ро┐ройрпБро│рпНро│рпЗ роЗро░рпБродрпНродро┐ройрпЗройрпН роЕродрпБро╡рпБроорпН роЕро╡ройродрпБ роЗройрпНройро░рпБро│рпЗ роЙрогро░рпНро╡рпБроорпН роЙропро┐ро░рпБроорпН роЙроЯроорпНрокрпБроорпН рооро▒рпНро▒рпБ роЙро▓рокрпНрокро┐ройро╡рпБроорпН рокро┤рпБродрпЗропро╛роорпН роЙрогро░рпНро╡рпИрокрпН рокрпЖро▒ро╡рпВро░рпНроирпНродро┐ро▒ро╡рпЗро▒ро┐ ропро╛ройрпБроорпН родро╛ройро╛ропрпКро┤ро┐роирпНродро╛ройрпЗ.

142

Lord of nitya sUris - SrI PerarulAlan on Garuda vAhanam - Kanchi

143

uNarvil umparoruvanai avanataruLAl uRaRporuTTu, en uNarvinuLLE iruttinEn, atuvum avanatu innaruLE uNarvum uyirum uDambum maRRu ulappinavum pazhutEyAm uNarvaip peRavUrntiRavERi yAnum tAnAyozhintAnE. (TiruvAimozhi, 8-8-3) Meaning:
In order to attain the Lord of nitya sUris, I fixed Him as the goal of my inner knowledge. Even this desire rose in my mind only due to His loving grace. He led me gradually to realize that seeking material objects, the life-breath, the physical body and other objects are useless. He did not stop with these, but took me further to realize my AtmA and then to realize that He is all; also that the term тАЬIтАЭ only indicates Himself and that He is the ultimate one being in all and the ultimate end.
SwAmi DeSikan has quoted this to emphasize that one performs prapatti only because of His grace and not by oneтАЩs own effort. Now, let us take up the second quotation, which too is from TiruvAimozhi: роЖро▒рпЖройроХрпНроХрпБ роиро┐ройрпН рокро╛родроорпЗ роЪро░рогро╛роХродрпН родроирпНродрпКро┤ро┐роирпНродро╛ропрпН роЙройроХрпНроХрпБ
роУро░рпН роХрпИроорпНрооро╛ро▒рпБроиро╛ройрпКройрпНро▒ро┐ро▓рпЗройрпН роОройродро╛ро╡ро┐ропрпБроорпН роЙройродрпЗ роЪрпЗро▒рпБроХрпКро│рпН роХро░рпБроорпНрокрпБроорпН рокрпЖро░рпБроЮрпНроЪрпЖроирпНроирпЖро▓рпБроорпН рооро▓ро┐родрогрпН роЪро┐ро░рпАро╡ро░роороЩрпНроХрпИ роиро╛ро▒рпБрокрпВроирпНродрогрпНродрпБро┤ро╛ропрпНроорпБроЯро┐ропро╛ропрпН родрпЖропрпНро╡роиро╛ропроХройрпЗ. ARenakku nin pAdamE caraNAakat tantozhintAi unakku
Or kaimmARu nAnonRilEn enatAviyum unatE cERukoL karumbum perum cennelum malitaN sirIvaramangai nARupUntaN tuzhAi muDiyAi deivanAyakanE. – TiruvAimozhi, 5-7-10

144

Meaning:
Oh deiva-nAyaka, the Lord Who adorns the garland of fragrant tuLasI, Who is stationed at the cool city of SirIvaramangai (VAnamAmalai) rich with the fields of sugar-cane and rice! You have yourself given Your feet as the fruit of my attainment and as the means for attaining it. For this mighty help, I do not have anything to give You in return, as even my AtmA too is Yours. SwAmi DeSikan concludes thus: тАЬрдЗрддреНрдпрд╛рджрд┐ роХро│ро┐ро▒рпНрокроЯро┐ропрпЗ рокрпНро░рокродрпНродро┐ропрпБроорпН роЕро╡ройроЯро┐ропро╛роХ ро╡роирпНродродрпЖройрпНро▒рпБ рдЕрдиреБрд╕рдВрдзреЗрдп роорпН тАЭ
тАЬityAdikaLiRpaDiyE prapattiyum avanaDiyAka vantatenRu anusandheyamтАЭ
In keeping with these and other pramANams, it should be borne in mind that the performance of prapatti too is due to Him.
SwAmi DeSikan cites another authority to emphasize that the prapanna should be aware that he is performing prapatti due to the LordтАЩs grace alone: роЗрокрпН рдкреНрд░рдХрд╛рд░ родрпНродрпИ, тАЬрд╕реНрд╡рдпрдВ рд╡рд╕реНрддреВ рдХреБрд░реНрд╡рдиреН рдЬрдирдорд┐рдордордХрд╕реНрдорд╛рддреН рд╕рд░рд╕рд┐рдЬрдкреНрд░рдХрд╛рд░реМ рдкреБрджреНрдорд╛рдпрд╛рд╕реНрддрд╡ рдЪ рдЪрд░рдгреМ рдирдГ рд╢рд░рдгрдпрдиреНтАЭ роОройрпНро▒рпБ ро▓роХрпНро╖рпНроорпА роХро▓рпНропро╛рогродрпНродро┐ро▓рпН роироорпНрооро╛ро┤рпНро╡ро╛ро░рпН рокро╛роЪрпБро░рооро╛роХ рокроЯрпНроЯро░рпН роЕро░рпБро│ро┐роЪрпН роЪрпЖропрпНродро╛ро░рпН. ip-prakArattai, тАЬsvayam vastU kurvan janamimamakasmAt sarasijaprakArau padmAyAstava ca caraNau na: SaraNayanтАЭ enRu lakshmI kalyANattil nammAzhvAr pAsuramAka bhaTTar aruLic seytAr. SwAmi DeSikan has explained that one should adopt the attitude of selflessness while doing any act laid down in SAstrAs, more particularly, when one performs prapatti. This is also emphasized by SrI ParAsara BhaTTar, in his work тАЬSrI LakshmI KalyANamтАЭ, through a quotation which he says is of SrI NammAzhvAr:

145

рд╕реНрд╡рдпрдВ рд╡рд╕реНрддреВ рдХреБрд░реНрд╡рдиреН рдЬрдирдорд┐рдордордХрд╕реНрдорд╛рддреН рд╕рд░рд╕рд┐рдЬрдкреНрд░рдХрд╛рд░реМ рдкреБрджреНрдорд╛рдпрд╛рд╕реНрддрд╡ рдЪ рдЪрд░рдгреМ рдирдГ рд╢рд░рдгрдпрдиреН svayam vastU kurvan janamimamakasmAt sarasijaprakArau padmAyAstava ca
caraNau na: SaraNayan Meaning:
(Oh Lord!) You grace me, who am a non-entity into a being and grant the lotus- like feet of Yours and that of Your Consort as a refuge to me! SwAmi DeSikan says, the sense of detachment is common to the performance of karma yogam etc. as well as the prapatti: родродрпНродрпНро╡роЬрпНроЮро╛ройроороЯро┐ропро╛роХ ро╡ро░рпБроХро┐ро▒ рдлрд▓рд╕рдЩреНрдЧ-рдХрд░реНрддреГрддреНрд╡-рддреНрдпрд╛рдЧ-рдкреВрд░реНрд╡рдХ рооро╛рой роЕроирпБро╖рпНроЯрпНроЯро╛роироорпН роиро┐ро╡рпНро░рпБродрпНродро┐- рдзрд░реНрдо роЩрпНроХро│ро╛рой рдХрд░реНрдордпрд╛реЛрдЧрд╛рджрд┐ роХро│ро┐ро▓рпБроорпН
рдкреНрд░рдкрджрди родрпНродро┐ро▓рпБроорпН родрпБро▓рпНропроорпН.
tattva-j~nAnamaDiyAka varukiRa phala-sanga-kartrtva-tyAga-pUrvakamAna anushThAnam nivrutti-dharmankaLAna karma-yogAdikaLilum prapadanattilum tulyam.
Any practice of rites based on the knowledge of essential nature of things will be devoid of self-centered outlook, that is, the doer will not have selfish attachment to the fruit of the act nor will he think he is the doer. This attitude of renunciation of phala and kartrtva is essential for performing karma yogam, bhakti yogam etc. The same applies to the performance of prapatti too, says SwAmi Desikan. He further says:
тАЬ роЙродрпНродро░ роХрпНро░рпБродрпНропродрпНродро┐ро▓рпН роЙрокро╛ропродрпНро╡ рддреНрдпрд╛рдЧ роорпН ро╡ро┐ро╢рпЗро╖ро┐родрпНродро┐ро░рпБроХрпНроХрпБроорпН. тАЭ тАЬuttara krutyattil upAyatva tyAga-m viSeshittirukkum.тАЭ During the post-prapatti life, the prapanna will do all good acts not as a means to moksham, but with the feeling of performing them as his duty. The feeling

146

of renunciation will be stronger while doing acts in the post-prapatti period. SwAmi DeSikan adds: тАЬрдкреНрд░рдкрджреНрдпреЗтАЭ
роОройрпНроХро┐ро▒ рд╡рд░реНрддрдорд╛рди-рдирд┐рд░реНрджреЗрд╢ роорпН рд╕рд╛рдЩреНрдЧ-рдЕрдиреБрд╖реНрдард╛рди- роХрпНро╖рогродрпНродрпИроХрпН роХро╛роЯрпНроЯрпБроХро┐ро▒родрпБ. тАЬprapadyeтАЭ enkiRa vartamAna-nirdeSam sAnga-anushThAna-kshaNattaik
kATTukiRatu. The term тАЬprapadyeтАЭ in the first part of the dvaya-mantram is in the present tense, meaning тАШI surrenderтАЩ. As this mantram is uttered at the moment of performing prapatti, the term тАЬprapadyeтАЭ in the mantram indicates prapatti with all its components.
As it is in the present sense, a doubt may arise: тАШтАЩDoes one have to perform prapatti till he leaves his present physical body?тАЩ Let us discover from SwAmi DeSikanтАЩs reply which follows next.
SwAmi DeSikan replies that prapatti is to be performed only once as it is done for a specific purpose: роЙрокро╛ро╕роиродрпНродро┐ро▓рпН тАЬрд╕рдХреГрддреН рдХреГрддрдГ рд╢рд╛рд╕реНрддреНрд░рд╛рд░реНрдердГтАЭ роОройрпНроХро┐ро▒ роирпНропро╛ропродрпНродро┐ро▒рпНроХрпБроЪрпН роЪро┐ро▓ ро╡роЪройроЩрпНроХро│ро╛ро▓рпН ро╡ро┐ро░рпЛродроорпН роЙрогрпНроЯро╛ропро┐ро▒рпНро▒рпБ. роЗроЩрпНроХрпБ роЕроирпБроХрпНро░ро╣роорпЗ роЙро│рпНро│родрпБ. роЗродрпБ, тАЬрд╕рдХреГрджреЗрд╡ рдкреНрд░рдкрдиреНрдирд╛рдптАЭ, тАЬрд╕рдХреГрджреЗрд╡ рд╣рд┐ рд╢рд╛рд╕реНрддреНрд░рд╛рд░реНрдердГтАЭ, тАЬрдпрдГ рд╕рдХреГрддреН рд╢рд░рдгрдВ рдЧрддрдГтАЭ, тАЬрдирдиреБ рдкреНрд░рдкрдиреНрдирдГ рд╕рдХреГрджреЗрд╡ рдирд╛рдетАЭ, тАЬрд╕рдХреГрддреН рдкреНрд░рд╛рд░реНрдердирд╛
рдорд╛рддреНрд░реЗрдгтАЭ, роЗродрпНропро╛родро┐роХро│ро╛ро▓рпБроорпН роХро╛роХро╛ро╕рпБро░ро╛родро┐ ро╡рпНро░рпБродрпНродро╛роирпНродроЩрпНроХро│ро╛ро▓рпБроорпН рд╕рд┐рджреНрдз роорпН. upASanattil, тАЬsakrt krta: SAsrArtha:тАЭ enkiRa nyAyattiRkuc cila vacanankaLAl virodham uNdAyiRRu. ingu anugrahamE uLLatu. itu тАЬsakrdeva prapannAyaтАЭ, тАЬsakrdeva hi SAstrArtha:тАЭ, тАЬya: sakrt SaraNam gata:тАЭ, тАЬnanu prapanna: sakrdeva nAthaтАЭ, тАЬsakrt prArthanA mAtreNaтАЭ ityAdikaLAlum kAkAsurAdi vruttAntankaLAlum siddham.
Here, by тАЬupASanamтАЭ, Swami DeSikan means bhakti yogam. He points out that in

147

the case of bhakti yogam, the rule laid down in the scripture, that is, an action specified for a particular goal has to be performed only once, is invalidated by certain specific rule meant only for the adoption of the bhakti yogam. This particular rule, which SwAmi DeSikan quotes, is from Karma mImAmsa. The full statement is: рд╕рдХреГрддреН рдХреГрддрдГ рд╢рд╛рд╕реНрддреНрд░рд╛рд░реНрдердГ рд╕рдХреГрддреНрддреБ рд╕реНрдпрд╛рддреН рдХреГрддрд╛рд░реНрдерддреНрд╡рд╛рджрдЩреНрдЧрд╡рддреН рее sakrut krta: SAstrArtha: sakrttu syAt krtArthatvAdangavat || –pUrva mImAmsa 11-1-22 Meaning:
An action, enjoined in the SAstra for a single objective, should be performed only once.
He points out that this general rule can not be applied in the case of bhakti yogam as it comes under some other rule exclusively laid down by the SAstra for those who choose this means. According to that rule, bhakti yogam has to be performed continuously till the attainment of the goal, that is, moksham. However, as regards prapatti, the rule quoted above is favourable to it and there is no need to do it again unlike in the case of bhakti yogam. SwAmi DeSikan says, this is confirmed from different examples like that of KaakAsura тАУ the Crow demon. He also mentions several quotations in support: рд╕рдХреГрджреЗрд╡ рдкреНрд░рдкрдиреНрдирд╛рдп рддрд╡рд╛рд╕реНрдореАрддрд┐ рдЪ рдпрд╛рдЪрддреЗред рдЕрднрдпрдВ рд╕рд░реНрд╡рднреВрддреЗрднреНрдпреЛ рджрджрд╛рдореНрдпреЗрддрджреНрд╡реНрд░рддрдВ рдордорее sakrdeva prapannAya tavAsmIti ca yAcate | abhayam sarvabhUtebhyo dadAmyetadvratam mama || (rAmAyaNam, 6-18-33)

148

Meaning:
If a person who performs prapatti only once saying, тАШI exist for YouтАЩ, I free him from fear from all beings. This is my vow. рд╕рдХреГрджреЗрд╡ рд╣рд┐ рд╢рд╛рд╕реНрддреНрд░рд╛рд░реНрдердГ рдХреГрддреЛрд╜рдпрдВ рддрд╛рд░рдпреЗрдиреНрдирд░рдореНред рдЙрдкрд╛рдпрд╛рдкрд╛рдпрд╕рдВрдпреЛрдЧреЗ рдирд┐рд╖реНрдардпрд╛ рд╣реАрдпрддреЗрд╜рдирдпрд╛рее sakrdeva SAstrArtha: krtoyam tArayennaram | upAyApAyasamyoge nishThayA hIyate anayA || (LakshmI tantram, 17-92) Meaning:
If a person performs prapatti just once, as laid down in the scripture, it will relieve him from the bondage of samsAra and bless him with moksham. рдХреБрдпреЛрдирд┐рд╖реНрд╡рдкрд┐ рд╕рдВрдЬрд╛рддреЛ рдпрдГ рд╕рдХреГрддреН рд╢рд░рдгрдВ рдЧрддрдГред рддрдВ рдорд╛рддрд╛рдкрд┐рддреГрд╣рдиреНрддрд╛рд░рдордкрд┐ рдкрд╛рддрд┐ рднрд╡рд╛рд░реНрддрд┐рд╣рд╛рее kuyonishvapi samjAto ya: sakrt SaraNam gata: | tam mAtApitru-hantAramapi pAti bhavArtihA || (Source not known) Meaning:
Even if a person may have been born in the lowest caste, if he performs prapatti just once, the Lord, Who is of the nature of removing the worldly suffering protects him even if he had committed the sin of killing his own parents. рдирдиреБ рдкреНрд░рдкрдиреНрдирдГ рд╕рдХреГрджреЗрд╡ рдирд╛рде

рддрд╡рд╛рдиреБрдХрдореНрдкреНрдпрдГ рд╕реНрдорд░рддрдГ рдкреНрд░рддрд┐рдЭрд╛рдВ

tavAhamsmIti ca yAcamAna: | tavAnukampya: smarata: pratij~nAm
madekavarjam kimidam vratam te || (stotra ratnam-64) Meaning:
Oh Lord, he who surrenders to You once saying тАЬI am YoursтАЭ becomes worthy of Your mercy. You remember the promise You made during Your incarnation as Rama. Is this resolve of Yours applicable to all excepting me? рд╕рдХреГрддреН рдкреНрд░рд╛рд░реНрдердирд╛рдорд╛рддреНрд░реЗрдг рдЕрдкреЗрдХреНрд╖рд┐рддрдВ рджрд╛рд╕реНрдпрддреАрддрд┐ рд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд╡рд╛рд╕рдкреВрд░реНрд╡рдХрдВ рдкреНрд░рд╛рд░реНрдердирдорд┐рддрд┐ рдпрд╛рд╡рддреНрее sakrt prArthanAmAtreNa apekshitam dAsytIti viSvAsapUrvakam
prArtanamiti yAvat || –SrIbhAshyakArar vAkyam Meaning:
Prapatti is a faith. That is, it is a prayer to the Lord with the faith that he will grant whatever we request from Him.
SwAmi DeSikan says these statements are all proved by the incidents such as the one involving the Crow demon тАУ kAkAsura, which is well known in the VaalmIki RaamAyaNa. It is now clear that prapatti is to be performed only once. The reference to the Crow demon was made by sItA while talking to HanumAn in the aSoka grove in Lanka.
Here, SwAmi DeSikan takes up a doubt that arises in the minds of people. They

150

point out that it is stated in Upanishads that prapatti is a yajna, that is, a sacrifice and it has an end like the avabhrtha snAnam as regards any sacrifice. That means there is continuity till the end of the sacrifice. But, they point out, in the case of prapatti, it has to be done only once, yet it has an end which is the death of the performer. This appears to be contradictory, they wonder. SwAmi DeSikan comes to clear this doubt now: роЗрокрпНрокроЯро┐ роХрпНро╖рогроХрпНро░рпБродрпНропрооро╛рой роирпНропро╛ро╕ ропро╛роХродрпНродрпБроХрпНроХрпБ роирпИро░рокрпЗроХрпНро╖рпНропроорпН родрпЛро▒рпНро▒рпБроХрпИроХрпНроХро╛роХ рдХреЗрд╡рд▓рдВ рднрдЧрд╡рддреН-рд╕рдВрдХрд▓реНрдк-рд╕рд╛рдзреНрдп рооро╛рой рооро░рогродрпНродрпИ рдЕрд╡рднреГрдердВ рпН роОройрпНроХро┐ро▒родрпБ. роЗродро▒рпНроХрпБ роЗро╡ройрпН роорпЗро▓ро┐ро░рпБроирпНродрпБ роЪрпЖропрпНропрпБроорпН рдЕрдиреБрдХреВрд▓-рд╡реГрддреНрддреНрдпрд╛рджрд┐ роХро│ро┐ро▓рпН роТройрпНро▒рпБроорпН роЗродро▒рпНроХрпБ роЕроЩрпНроХрооройрпНро▒рпБ роОройрпНроХрпИропро┐ро▓рпЗ родро╛родрпНрокро░рпНропроорпН.
ippaDi kshaNakruthyamAna nyAsa yAgattukku nairapekshyam tORRukaikkAka kevalam bhagavat-sankalpa-sAdhyamAna maraNattai avabhrtham enkiRatu. itaRku ivan mEliruntu seyyum anukUla-vrttyAdikaLil onRum itaRku angamanRu enkaiyilE tAtparyam.
nyAsam or prapatti which is a sacrifice, takes just a moment to perform and complete and it has to be done only once. Besides, it does not require any other component. This apparent contradiction is resolved thus: As the scripture states, only the prapannaтАЩs end life is the closure of this prapatti yajna. However, the death is not in his hands, it may be asked. It is explained, his death occurs as per the LordтАЩs will alone. The intention of describing his death as the avabhrtha snAnam, the ceremonial bath taken after a sacrifice is finished.
SwAmi DeSikan further says: The good services being done by the cetana who has performed the momentary prapatti will not form part of prapatti, as prapatti does not need any supplementary acts. That is why the death of the prapanna is described as the avabhrtha snAnam. SwAmi DeSikan goes further:

151

роЗрокрпНрокрпВро░рпНро╡ рдЦрдгреНрдб родрпНродро┐ро▓рпН рокрпНро░роХро╛роЪро┐родрпНрод рокро░роирпНропро╛ро╕родрпНродрпИ роЕроирпБро╖рпНроЯрпНроЯро┐роХрпНроХрпБрооро╡ройрпБроХрпНроХрпБ рддрддреНрддреНрд╡- рдЭрд╛рдирд╛рджрд┐-рд╕рдВрдкрд╛рджрдирдВ рдкреВрд░реНрд╡-рдХреГрддреНрдпрдореН . рдЖрдиреБрдХреВрд▓реНрдп рд╕рдВрдХрд▓реНрдкрд╛рджрд┐ рддрддреНрдХрд╛рд▓-рдХреГрддреНрдп роорпН. ро╢рпНро╡ропроорпН
рокрпНро░ропрпЛроЬроирооро╛рой рдирд┐рд░рдкрд╛рд░рд╛рдз роХрпИроЩрпНроХро░рпНропроорпН роЙродрпНродро░ рдХреГрддреНрдп роорпН.

ippUrva khaNDattil prakAsitta bharanyAsattai anushTTikkumavanukku tattva- j~nAnAdi-sampAdanam pUrva-krtyam, AnukUlya sankalpAdi tatkAla-krytyam. svayam-prayOjanamAna kainkaryam uttara krtyam. Here, SwAmi DeSikan explains, before a person adopts prapatti he should approach an AcArya and acquire knowledge about tattvA-s, bhagavad bhakti etc. This is essential.

Approach a sadAcArya to acquire knowledge HH 45th paTTam SrImat azhagiya singar At the time of doing prapatti, he should be firm to do things that will please the Lord and take a pledge that he will not do things which are considered sins.

152

Again, after he adopts prapatti, he should not engage in activities with traces of sin; he should continue to perform daily and occasional karmA-s with an attitude of these being his services to the Lord and not for any personal benefits. SwAmi Desikan continues further: рдкреВрд░реНрд╡-рдХреГрддреНрдп-рд╡рд┐рдХрд▓ ройрпН рдЕрдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░рд┐ роЕро▓рпНро▓ройрпН. рддрддреНрдХрд╛рд▓-рдХреГрддреНрдп-рд╡рд┐рдХрд▓ ройрпН рдХреГрддрдХреГрддреНрдп ройро▓рпНро▓ройрпН. рдЙрддреНрддрд░- рдХреГрддреНрдп-рд╡рд┐рдХрд▓ ройрпН рдХреГрддрд╛рд░реНрде ройро▓рпНро▓ройрпН. роЗрокрпНрокроЯро┐ рд╡рд┐рдХрд▓ ро░ро╛ройро╡ро░рпНроХро│рпБроорпН тАЬрдХрдердВрдЪрд┐рджреБрдкрдХрд╛рд░реЗрдг рдХреГрддреЗрдиреИрдХреЗрди рддреБрд╖реНрдпрддрд┐тАЭ роОройрпНроХро┐ро▒рокроЯро┐ропрпЗ рдХреГрддрдЭ ройро╛рой ро╢ро░рогрпНропройрпБроЯрпИроп роХрпНро░рпБрокрпИропро╛ро▓рпЗ
рдХреНрд░рдореЗрдг рокрпВро░рпНрогро░ро╛ро╡ро╛ро░рпНроХро│рпН. pUrva-krtya-vikalan adhikAri allan. tatkAla-krtya-vikalan krta-krtyanallan. uttara-krtya-vikalan krtArthan allan. ippaDi vikalarAnavarkaLum тАЬkathamcidupakAreNa krtenaikena tushyatiтАЭ enkiRapaDiyE krtaj~nanAna SaraNyanuDaiya krupaiyAlE krameNa pUrNarAvarkaL. SwAmi DeSikan says, a person who does not earn the necessary knowledge stated earlier before prapatti, he becomes ineligible for adopting prapatti. Similarly, in case whatever is required to be done at the time of performing prapatti, is not done by anyone, he becomes unfit to adopt prapatti. Again, the person after performing prapatti does not conduct him-self as expected will not be considered to be on the right path.
However, even persons with such shortcomings will, as time passes, turn perfect by the grace of the Lord, Who remains grateful even for a small good act done to Him. SwAmi DeSikan shows an authoritative scriptural statement in support: тАЬрд╕рдХреГрдЬреНрдЬрдкреНрддреЗрди рдордиреНрддреНрд░реЗрдгтАЭ
роОройрпНро▒рпБ ро╕ро╛родрпНропроХро┐ родроирпНродрпНро░родрпНродро┐ро▓рпН роЪрпКройрпНройродрпБ роЗроЩрпНроХрпБроорпН родрпБро▓рпНропрооро┐ро▒рпЗ.

153

sakrt japtena mantreNaтАЭ enRu sAtyaki tantrattil sonnatu ingum tulyamiRE. It is stated in the scripture named тАШsAtayaki tantramтАЩ that the person who does prapatti uttering once the dvaya mantram will attain the greatest bliss. This is equally applicable here too. SwAmi Desikan gives a few more quotes in support: рднрд╡ рд╢рд░рдгрдорд┐рддреАрд░рдпрдиреНрддрд┐ рдпреЗ рд╡реИ bhava SaraNamitIrayanti ye vai This quote is a part of a Slokam from SrI VishNupurANam. We shall see the full Slokam: рдХрдорд▓рдирдпрди рд╡рд╛рд╕реБрджреЗрд╡ рд╡рд┐рд╖реНрдгреЛ рдзрд░рдгрд┐рдзрд░рд╛рдЪреНрдпреБрдд рд╢рдЩреНрдЦрдЪрдХреНрд░рдкрд╛рдгреЗред рднрд╡ рд╢рд░рдгрдорд┐рддреАрд░рдпрдиреНрддрд┐ рдпреЗ рд╡реИ рд╡реНрдпрдЬ рднрдЯ рджреВрд░рддрд░реЗрдг рддрд╛рдирдкрд╛рдкрд╛рдиреНрее kamalanayana vAsudeva vishNo dharaNidharAcyuta Sankha-cakra-pANe | bhava SaraNamitIrayanti ye vai vyaja bhaTa dUratareNa tAnapApAn || —VishNu PurANam, 3-7-33 Meaning:

Oh the Lord of Kaanci! тАЬsakrt uccaritam yena hari: ityakshara dvayamтАЭ enkiRapadiyE laghuvAna iraNDu aksharankaLai uccarikka, iTTapaDai kal paDaiyAnAl, gurutaramAna iv-vAkya dvayattai uccarittavanukku itu kETka vENDumO? We have seen how the Lord considers Himself grateful to the cetana for just doing a minute bit of good act that pleases Him. He does not stop there, but comes forward to complete the effect of the cetanaтАЩs prapatti so that he achieves the goal for which he did the prapatti, i.e., moksham. When the SAstrAs assure the fruit in full for uttering the dvaya mantram just once, is it not justified that even if there are shortcomings in the case of a prapanna, he will in due course attain the benefit in full?

When the sattva quality dominates in a person, all perturbation in his mind due to rAjasa and tAmasa qualities will disappear. Thereafter, when he adopts total surrender at the LordтАЩs feet, the purpose for which he performed the prapatti will bring benefit to him at the exact time as he desired. paramAtmA ca tenaiva sAdhyate purushottama: || —ahirbhudnya Samhita,37-25, 26, 27 Meaning:
Whatever object desired, by whatsoever person and whatever cannot be obtained by other means, and that moksham from which abode there is no return and which cannot be attained by karma yogam, j~nAna yogam or bhakti yogam, all these fruits are obtained, Oh great Sage, by those who strive for these goals by performing prapatti. The Supreme Self is attained only by prapatti. Meaning: SrI, the Consort of the Lord, removes the obstacles to adopting the means of prapatti for the persons who approach Her. She also makes their qualities fit enough to do service to the Lord. She listens to the plea made by them trembling out of fear, тАЬOh Devi please reach us, the sinners as we are, to the feet of the LordтАЭ. She makes the Lord to listen to their plea. She is easily approachable by all who are eager to survive. She approaches the Lord for the sake of those who approached Her. The Lord Who never parts with His Consort even for a moment sees that His auspicious qualities would become meaningful only if He protects the jIvA-s who approach Him and His Consort. He establishes His title of being the Greatest Protector by inducing his devotees in prapatti and accepts them under His feet for according protection to them. ippaDi sarva purushArtthankaLaiyum sAdhikkavaRRAna upAyam ingu etaRkAka? enna, тАЬkaNDu kETTuтАЭ enkiRa pATTinpaDiyE kshudra-pryOjanangkaLODu tuvakkaRRa purushArttha viSeshattaik kATTukiRatu, uttara khaNDam. A query arises: It has been stated that the means of prapatti is capable of getting all sorts of objectives. For what purpose such a means has been mentioned here in this dvayam? The answer is: While there are innumerable objectives to be attained in this mundane world that are not ever lasting, there

is, however, one which is completely different from such worldly objectives and which lasts for ever. That is moksham which is revealed by the later part of the dvaya mantram

The Divine vision of BHagavAn with SrI Deities at SrI MaTham, Chembur In this regard, SwAmi DeSikan refers to a verse from TiruvAimozhi of SrI NammAzhvAr, with a quote, тАЬkaNDu kETTuтАЭ. oNtoDiyAL tirumakaLum niumE nilA niRpa kaNDacatir kaNDozhintEn aDaintEn un tiruvaDiyE.
—TiruvAimozhi, 4-9-10 Meaning:
The pleasures of five senses of seeing, hearing, touching, smelling and tasting and also, the unlimited but inferior enjoyment of oneтАЩs own Self (AtmAnubhavam) which is not capable of being realized by the senses, have been given up by me. I have now witnessed the beautiful vision of both You and Sri together and attained Your divine feet. Here ends the discussion on the earlier part (pUrva bhAgam) of dvayam. SwAmi DeSikan takes up the latter part (uttara bhAgam) of the mantram. THE SECOND PART OF DVAYAM The significance of the term тАШSrImatтАЩ SwAmi DeSikan now takes up for discussion the latter part (uttara bhAgam) of the dvaya mantram, i.e., тАЬSrImate nArAyaNAya nama:тАЭ. First comes the term тАЬSrimateтАЭ- which literally means тАШassociated with SrI- LakshmIтАЩ. This term precedes the LordтАЩs name, тАШnArayaNaтАЩ Who is ever inseparably united with His Consort, SrI. Along with Her, the Lord stands as тАШSeshiтАЩ тАУ the Master. Both jointly accept the kainkaryam-s, services, rendered by the cetana in SrIvaikuNTham, the highest Abode. This fact has been talked about by AzhvAr and in RaamAyaNa as well as in the stotra ratnam of SrI ALavantAr which are referred to by SwAmi DeSikan: роЗродро┐ро▓рпН тАШрд╢реНрд░реАрдорддреНтАЩ рд╢рдмреНрдж роорпН

Meaning:

AzhvAr expresses his longing to join the Lord, not Him alone, but with His Consort, Lakshmi. Hence, SwAmi DeSikan highlights the importance of serving the Divine Couple together and not merely the Lord alone. This is signified by the term тАШSrImatтАЩ in the latter part of the dvaya mantram. cErttiyilE kainkarya-pratisambandhiyAyk koNDu nitya-yuktamAi niRkiRa nilaiyaik kATTukiRatu. тАУ The term тАШSrImatтАЩ in the latter part of the dvaya mantram reveals the fact that SrI is inseparably ever with the Lord in the ultimate state of SrIvaikuNTham receiving the services of the mukta jIvan, as She is at the stage of performance of prapatti by the jIvan. SwAmi DeSikan raises an important point: рд╢реНрд░реБрддреНрдпрд╛рджрд┐ роХро│ро┐ро▓рпЗ ро╕ро░рпНро╡-ро╡ро┐ро╢ро┐ро╖рпНроЯройрпН рокрпНро░ро╛рокрпНропройро╛роХроЪрпН роЪрпКро▓рпНро▓ро┐ропро┐ро░рпБроХрпНроХ, SrutyAdikaLilE sarva-viSishTan prApyanAkakc colliyirukka тАУ Scriptures like Upanishads establish that the Lord alone is the goal to be experienced as He is the sole ruler of both leelA and nitya vibhUtis. When that is the case, here in the dvayam, how He is said to be ever with His Consort, SrI? SwAmi DeSikan gives the answer also. When it is said the Lord nArAyaNa, combined with Sri, is the fruit, it should be understood that there is nothing

169

superior than the Divine Couple (the Lord and Sri); Both are Seshi:-Master- Mistress Couple. This is the significant message conveyed by the term тАШSrImatтАЩ in both parts of the dvaya mantram. Here it is specifically mentioned to highlight this combined ownership of all. fitting to understand Her being worshipped and served by every one. (Note:- The third quote above is from a work named, тАШshaDartha sankshepamтАЩ of somAsiyANDAn. Here are some points regarding somAsiyANDAn. He was an important disciples of SrI rAmAnuja. He wrote a commentary on SrIbhAshyam, titled, тАШSrI-bhAshya-vivrttiтАЩ. He also wrote a few works such as shaDartha sankshepam and guruguNAvaLi, as mentioned in the literary works of pUrvAchArya-s. somAsiyANDAn was also known as SrI rAma miSra.) SwAmi DeSikan again deals with another doubt that may arise in our minds. The doubt is: Even after the term тАШSrImateтАЩ itself denotes the Lord-His Spouse (SrI) combination itself is the ultimate goal of us all, why should there be yet another term, тАШnArAyaNaтАЩ here? SwAmi DeSikan seeks to clear this doubt: ро╕ро░рпНро╡-ро╢рпЗро╖ро┐ропро╛рой родродрпНродрпНро╡роорпН рдкреНрд░рдзрд╛рди-рдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрдп рооро╛ройро╛ро▓рпБроорпН рдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрддрд╛ ро╡ро┐ройрпН рд╕реНрд╡рд░реВрдкрдВ роорпБродро▓ро╛рой ро╕ро░рпНро╡ ро╡ро┐ро╢рпЗро╖рогроЩрпНроХро│рпБроорпН рдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрдп-рдХреЛрдЯрд┐-рдШрдЯрд┐рдд роЩрпНроХро│ро╛ропрпН роиро┐ро▒рпНроХро┐ро▒ роиро┐ро▓рпИропрпИроХрпН роХро╛роЯрпНроЯрпБроХро┐ро▒родрпБ роЗроЩрпНроХрпБро▒рпНро▒ роиро╛ро░ро╛ропрог ро╢рокрпНродроорпН.
sarva-SeshiyAna tattvam pradhAna-prApyamAnAlum prAptAvin svarUpam mutalAna sarva viSehaNangaLum prApya-koTi-ghaTitankaLAi niRkiRa nilaiyaik kATTukiRatu inguRRa nArAyaNa Sabdam. deSa-kAla-purusha-bhedattAlE paNDu bahuvidhamAna AnukUlya- prAtikUlyAdikaLai aDaintavai sarva-upAdhikaLum kazhinthavanukku svAmi-

vibhUtiyAna AkArattAlE atyanta-anukUlangkaLAi irukkum.
While being in this world of samsAra, the cetana experiences certain things as enjoyable and certain other things troublesome. The same thing that appears favourable at one place or time, will appear unfavourable at another place or time. It may be enjoyable for a person and disgusting for another. All these differences are due to each oneтАЩs previous karmAs - puNya and pApa. For a mukta, all his previous karmA and the physical body along with the senses which he got due to those karmAs will disappear. In that state of mukta, any object he sees will appear to him as belonging to the Lord and to be under His control. Hence, any object will appear favourable to him. рдЕрдирдиреНрддрд╛рддреНрдорд╛ роХрпНроХро│рпБроХрпНроХрпБроорпН ро╡ро░рпБроорпН роРро╢рпНро╡ро░рпНроп-роЖродрпНрооро╛роирпБрокро╡ ро░ро╕родрпНродрпИ роОро▓рпНро▓ро╛роорпН роЪрпЗро░рокрпН рокро╛ро░рпНродрпНродро╛ро▓рпБроорпН рокро░ро┐рокрпВро░рпНрог- рдмреНрд░рд╣реНрдорд╛рдиреБрднрд╡-рд░реВрдк рооро╛рой родро┐ро░рпБрокрпНрокро╛ро▒рпНроХроЯро▓ро┐ро▓рпН роТро░рпБ родро┐ро╡ро▓рпИроХрпНроХрпБроорпН рокро▒рпНро▒ро╛родрпБ.
anantAtmAkkaLukkum varum aiSvarya-AtmAnubhava rasattai ellAm cErappArttAlum paripUrNa-brahmAnubhava-rUpamAna tiruppARkaDalil oru tivalaikkum paRRAtu. In this universe, there are countless Atma-s. Suppose all of them together enjoy all the pleasures available in all the worlds up to the Brahma lokam and the enjoyment still greater in the enjoyment of oneтАЩs own Self, known as kaivalya mukti. All these put together will be like a small drop in the Milky Ocean compared to the bliss that a mukta gets while enjoying the closest proximity of the Lord in SrIvaikuNTham.

In SrIvaikuNTham, nitya-s and mukta-s render special services to the Lord who

173

is seated on the divine seat. This has been described in the Upanishads. The Lord also appears in His unique divine form receiving their services. His unique divine form is indicated in this term of тАШnArAyaNaтАЩ, which should be specially noted by us. рдкрд░реНрдпрдЩреНрдХ рд╡рд┐рджреНрдпрд╛ paryanka vidyA тАУ There are different varieties in bhakti yogam, one of which is paryanka vidyA. This is found in KaushItaki Upanishad, where all the aspects of the LordтАЩs presence in SrIvaikuNTham are described in detail. In the term тАШnArayaNaтАЩ one should think of this, says Swami DeSikan. In SrIvaikuNTham, there is a place for the mukta-s, specifically meant for them. It is the space between the feet of the Lord and the lotus that is supporting the feet. kadA puna: Sankha-rathAnga-kalpaka- dhvajAravindAnkuSa-vajra-lAnchanam | trivikrama svaccaraNAmbujadvayam madIyamUrdhAnam-alankarishyati || –stotraratnam -31 Meaning:

kalpaka-tree, flag, lotus, hook and thunder-bolt, adorn my head?
The latter part of the dvaya mantram consists of three terms, that is: тАЬSrImate nArAyaNAya nama:тАЭ. Of these, the terms тАШSrImateтАЩ and тАШnArAyaNaтАЩ have been discussed so far. These show the Lord as the Master to all and in every way He is of limitless pleasantness to all. Then comes the dative (fourth- case) suffix тАШAyaтАЩ attached to тАЬnArAyaNaтАЭ. Swami DeSikan now takes up to explain this. It indicates тАШfor nArAyaNaтАЩ, that is, тАШexclusively meant for nArAyaNaтАЩ. This is further extended to mean, тАШone is Sesha to HimтАЩ. SwAmi DeSikan puts it this way: роЗрокрпНрокроЯро┐ ро╕ро░рпНро╡-ро╢рпЗро╖ро┐родрпНро╡-ро╕ро░рпНро╡-рокрпНро░роХро╛ро░-роиро┐ро░родро┐ро╢роп- рднреЛрдЧреНрдпрддреНрд╡ роЩрпНроХро│рпИ рдкреНрд░рдзрд╛рди рооро╛роХрокрпН рокро┐ро░роХро╛роЪро┐рокрпНрокро┐роХрпНроХро┐ро▒ рдкрдж роЩрпНроХро│ро┐ро▓рпН рдЪрддреБрд░реНрдереА рддрд╛рджрд░реНрдереНрдп рооро╛родрпНро░родрпНродрпИроЪрпН роЪрпКройрпНройро╛ро▓рпН роХрпАро┤рпНроЪрпН роЪрпКро▓рпНро▓рпБроХро┐ро▒ роЙрокро╛ропродрпНродрпЛроЯрпБ роЪрпЛрпНродрпНродро┐ропро┐ро▓рпНро▓ро╛роорпИропро╛ро▓рпЗ тАж ..

Thus, the terms SrImate and nArayaNa point out both SrI and nArAyana are the Masters enjoying wonderful pleasures in all ways. When such is the position, if the fourth-case suffix (Aya) is said to indicate the meaning тАШservant only to HimтАЩ, it does not go with the means (upAyam) of surrender in the earlier part of the mantra, тАЬSrIman nArayaNa caraNau SaraNam prapadyeтАЭ. Moreover, the jIva is ever a Sesha, is it not? There is no need to specify this separately. Hence, we must find out what is the fitting meaning for the suffix, тАШAyaтАЩ. nitya siddhamAna it tAdarthyartattukku anurUpamAi sAdhyamAi nirupAdhika-

anubhava-parIvAhamAi vaiparItyAdi-rahitamAi sarva-deSAdi-yogyamAna yathA-abhimata-sarvavidha-kainkaryattaiyum kATTukiRatu.
This dative (fourth case suffix), meaning тАШexisting for nArAyaNaтАЩ, indicates the тАШserviceтАЩ the cetana has to render in all states and at all times to the Lord. This is an eternal fact (nitya siddha). This is obviously to be attained. The cetana, once all his karmAs are gone, naturally experiences the Lord and does the services to Him thereby enjoying the bliss in the SrIvaikuNTham. All the perversions like тАШI and mineтАЩ which he had earlier having disappeared, the cetana freely engaged in pure services of all kinds as he likes. This sort of kainkaryam is indicated by the dative (fourth-case) suffix, тАШAyaтАЩ. Such a service is prayed for by the cetana at the time of prapatti, says SwAmi Desikan: роЗродройрпН рдкреНрд░рд╛рд░реНрде ройрпИроХрпНроХрпБ роЗроЩрпНроХрпЗ роТро░рпБ рдХреНрд░рд┐рдпрд╛рдкрдж роорпН рдЕрдзреНрдпрд╛рд╣рд╛рд░реНрдп роорпН. itan prArthanaikku ingE oru kriyApadam adhyAhAryam.

Meaning:
Oh Lord, Who is ever present in the highest Abode of SrIvaikuNTham of

179

unlimited bliss! It is true, I am You, as You are present every where and in every thing. It is Your order that I am in this hell-like world. Hence, whether I attain the SrIvaikuNTham or the hell, it does not matter. However, I fear; when I realize that You are in me, I fear to remain in this hell-like world. Therefore, please grant me Your feet!

The Abode of unlimited bliss! - SrI VaikuNTham роЪрпВро┤рпНроЪрпНроЪро┐роЮро╛ройроЪрпН роЪрпБроЯро░рпКро│ро┐ропро╛роХро┐ роОройрпНро▒рпБроорпН роПро┤рпНроЪрпНроЪро┐роХрпН роХрпЗроЯро┐ройрпНро▒ро┐ роОроЩрпНроХрогрпБроорпН роиро┐ро▒рпИроирпНрод роОроирпНродро╛ропрпН родро╛ро┤рпНроЪрпНроЪро┐ рооро▒рпНро▒рпЖроЩрпНроХрпБроорпН родро╡ро┐ро░рпНроирпНродрпБ роиро┐ройрпН родро╛ро│ро┐рогрпИроХрпНроХрпАро┤рпН ро╡ро╛ро┤рпНроЪрпНроЪро┐ ропро╛ройрпНроЪрпЗро░рпБроорпН ро╡роХрпИ роЕро░рпБро│ро╛ропрпН ро╡роирпНродрпЗ.

Oh Lord, You are pervading all objects, whether animate or inanimate! In order that I escape the decay by continuing here, You must appear now before me in flesh and blood to enable me to take refuge under Your feet. Here is a quote from SaraNAgati gadyam: тАж..рдкреНрд░реАрддрд┐рдХрд╛рд░рд┐рдд рдЕрд╢реЗрд╖рд╛рд╡рд╕реНрдереЛрдЪрд┐рдд рдЕрд╢реЗрд╖рд╢реЗрд╖рддреИрдХрд░рддрд┐рд░реВрдк рдирд┐рддреНрдпрдХрд┐рдЩреНрдХрд░реЛ рднрд╡рд╛рдирд┐ ….prItikArita aSeshAvasthocita aSesha SeshataikaratirUpa nitya kinkaro bhavAni

The cetana while performing prapatti, prays for the highest benefit, that is, moksham. When he will get it? He can get it only after all types of impediments including ignorance, karmAs etc. are dispensed with completely, is it not? He has also enjoyed various types of materialistic pleasures in this world. He enjoyed them, thinking that he was an independent person, he was acting for his own benefit and for his own enjoyment. These were wrong thoughts. Now in the state of moksham, all these previous thoughts have been replaced by the right thinking that whatever he does is done by the Lord Himself for His own benefit. This state of mind is highlighted by the term тАЬnama:тАЭ here. SwAmi DeSikan endorses this with a quote from thiruvAimozhi, родройроХрпНроХрпЗропро╛роХ роОройрпИроХрпНроХрпКро│рпНро│рпБроорпН tanakkEyAka enaikkoLLum Let us consider the verse in full: роОройроХрпНроХрпЗропро╛роЯрпНроЪрпЖропрпН роОроХрпНроХро╛ро▓родрпНродрпБроорпН роОройрпНро▒рпБ роОройрпН рооройроХрпНроХрпЗ ро╡роирпНродрпБ роЗроЯрпИро╡рпАроЯро┐ройрпНро▒ро┐ рооройрпНройро┐ родройроХрпНроХрпЗропро╛роХ роОройрпИроХрпНроХрпКро│рпНро│рпБроорпН роИродрпЗ роОройроХрпНроХрпЗроХрогрпНрогройрпИ ропро╛ройрпН роХрпКро│рпНроЪро┐ро▒рокрпНрокрпЗ. enakkE ATcey ekkAlattum enRu en manakkE vantu iDaivIDinRi manni

tanakkEyAka enaikkoLLum ItE enakkE kaNNanai yAn koLciRappE. (tiruvAimozhi, 2-9-4) Meaning:
The best benefit I seek from the Lord is: He must enter into my mind saying, тАШYou shall serve Me all timesтАЩ and stay put in me continuously without even a minuteтАЩs break; this very acceptance of me as His own will befit the nature of my AtmA.
This verse is considered by our pUvAcAriar-s as the crown of this group of ten verses. The Lord could ask the AzhvAr, тАШServeтАЩ; or тАШServe MeтАЩ; or тАШServe Me aloneтАЩ; but the AzhvAr will not be satisfied. Hence, the AzhvAr says тАШThe Lord must ask him to serve Him for everтАЩ; he insists that the Lord should not only enter into his mind, but should stay put there for ever, that too, uninterruptedly. He says, such a gesture of the Lord alone will befit his Atma svarUpam. The AzhvAr says, it is the greatest favour that he seeks from the Lord.
SwAmi DeSikan points out that whatever the AzhvAr has shown in his pAsuram quoted above is indicated by the term, тАЬnama:тАЭ. He further says: роЗродрпБро╡рпБроорпН родро┐ро░рпБроороирпНродрпНро░родрпНродро┐ро▓рпН ро╕рпВроХрпНро╖рпНроо ропрпЛроЬройрпИропро┐ро▓рпН рокрпЛро▓рпЗ роЗро░рогрпНроЯрпБ роОро┤рпБродрпНродрпБроорпН роЗро░рогрпНроЯрпБ рдкрдж рооро╛ропрпН рдЕрдзреНрдпрд╛рд╣рд░рд┐ родрпНрод рдХреНрд░рд┐рдпрд╛-рдкрдж родрпНродрпЛроЯрпЗ роЕроирпНро╡ропро┐родрпНродрпБ роТро░рпБ ро╡ро╛роХрпНропрооро╛роХро┐ро▒родрпБ. ituvum tirumanrattil sUkshma yOjanaiyil pOlE iraNDu ezhuttum iraNDu padamAi adhyAharitta kriyA-padatODE anvayittu oru vAkyamAkiRatu. As stated in the previous chapter on тАШtirumantrAdhikAramтАЩ (Please see SrI HayagrIvan series e-book # 52 at http://www.srihayagrivan.org), here too, the term тАЬnama:тАЭ has to be explained after splitting it in to two words, тАЬnaтАЭ and тАЬma:тАЭ. The words lined up in the dvaya mantram will mean thus: The first part (pUrva bhAgam): SrImat together with the Consort, тАЬSrIтАЭ;

184

The suffix, тАШmatupтАЩ - тАЬSrIтАЭ remains inseparable; nArAyaNa having qualities for extending protection; caraNau the divinely auspicious form of the Supreme Lord; SaraNam being an тАШupAyamтАЩ (means) prapadye prapatti is done only once as a tool to endear Him; The first person termination тАУ the qualification of the person who does the prapatti. The latter part (uttara bhAgam): SrImate The Lord who is the Master of all, together with His Consort, accepts the service offered; nArAyaNa Being pleasing in all respects; Aya to do service as He desires; nama: serving Him without any ego; syAt praying for doing pure service to Him. akincanAna nAn SrImAnAna nArAyaNan tiruvaDikaLil sarva-vidha-dosha- rahitamAi sva-abhimatamAna sarva-vidha-kainkarya-vargattaiyum peRukaikku SrIman nArAyaNan tiruvaDikaLaiyE upAyamAkak koNDu yathoktamAna Atma- rakshA-bhara-samarppaNam paNNukiREn enRu oru vAkyArtthamAkiRatu. The dvaya mantram comprises three sentences - the first part forms a single sentence, while the latter part contains two sentences. These three sentences taken together gives this message: тАЬBeing the servant of no one else other than the Lord, having no resources like bhakti yogam, I surrender the responsibility of the protecting me at the feet of nArAyaNa who is the Lord of all, who is inseparable from LakshmI and in order that I may obtain rendering all kinds of service, in all places, at all times and in all states.тАЭ роЗро╡рпН роЕро░рпНродрпНрод-роЕроирпБро╕роирпНродро╛роироорпН роЙрокро╛роп родроЪрпИропро┐ро▓рпН рд╕рдХреГ родрпНродро╛ропрпН рдХреГрдд-рдХреГрддреНрдпрддрд╛- ро╣рпЗродрпБро╡ро╛ропро┐ро░рпБроХрпНроХрпБроорпН.
iv arthta-anusandhAnam upAya dasaiyil sakrttAi krta-krtyatA-hEtuvAyirukkum.
In this way, one should keep in mind the meaning of the dvaya mantram while performing the one-time prapatti. By this he remains as having executed what he is expected to do. ро╕рпНро╡ропроорпН рокрпНро░ропрпЛроЬроирооро╛рой роЙродрпНродро░ роХрпНро░рпБродрпНропродрпНродро┐ро▓рпН рд╕рджрд╛ ро╡ро╛ропрпН рдХреГрддрд╛рд░реНрдерддрд╛тАУ ро╣рпЗродрпБро╡ро╛ропро┐ро░рпБроХрпНроХрпБроорпН. svayam prayOjanamAna uttara krtyattil sadAvAi krtArthatA-hEtuvAyirukkum.
During the post-prapatti life, he should remain keeping in his mind this meaning of the dvaya mantram, which itself is the fruit of the prapatti performed by him. рокрпНро░ропрпЛроЬроиродрпНро╡роорпБроорпН роЗро░рогрпНроЯрпБ роЗроЯродрпНродро┐ро▓рпБроорпН роЕроироирпНропро╛ро░рпНро╣-ро╢рпЗро╖родрпНро╡роорпБроорпН рд╕рд┐рджреНрдзрд┐ роХрпНроХро┐ро▒родрпБ. роЗрокрпНрокроЯро┐ роЗроЩрпНроХрпБроороЩрпНроХрпБроорпН родро┐ро░рпБрооро╛ро▓ройрпНро▒ро┐ роЗройрпНроорпИ роХрогрпНроЯро╡ройрпН рджреНрд╡рдпрдирд┐рд╖реНрда ройрпН.
itil pUrva-khaNDattil ananya-upAyatvamum uttara-khaNDattil ananya- prayOjanatvamum iraNDu iDattilum ananyArha-Seshatvamum siddhikkiRatu. ippaDi ingum angum tirumAlanRi inmai kaNDavan dvayanishThan. As the first part of the dvaya mantram highlights the prapatti, the prapannan needs no other means except the LordтАЩs feet. As the latter part highlights the service at the LordтАЩs feet, it is clear that the prapannan should not accept any other benefit except the service at the LordтАЩs feet. Considering both parts together, it becomes clear that he is a servant to the Lord alone and to no one else. Thus a person who has understood that the Lord and His Consort, SrI together alone are the upayam and the benefit, emerges as the one who has attained the position as stated in the dvaya mantram. SwAmi DeSikan concludes this chapter on dvayAdhikAtam with a Tamizh verseтАЭ роОройрпНройродрпБропро╛ройрпН роЪрпЖропрпНроХро┐ройрпНро▒рпЗройрпН роОройрпНройро╛родро╛ро░рпБроХрпНроХрпБ роЗройрпНройроЯро┐роорпИ родроирпНродро│ро┐рокрпНрокро╛ройрпН роЗроорпИропрпЛро░рпН ро╡ро╛ро┤рпБроорпН рокрпКройрпНройрпБро▓роХро┐ро▓рпН родро┐ро░рпБро╡рпБроЯройрпЗ роЕрооро░рпНроирпНрод роиро╛родройрпН рокрпБройро▓ро╛ро░рпБроорпН рокрпКро┤ро┐ро▓ро░роЩрпНроХроорпН родро┐роХро┤ рооройрпНройро┐родрпН родройрпНройроХро▓роорпН роЕроХро▓ро╛род родроХро╡ро╛ро▓рпЛроЩрпНроХрпБроорпН родроХро╡рпБроЯройрпЗ родройрпНроХро░рпБроороорпН родро╛ройрпЗропрпЖрогрпНрогро┐ роЕройрпНройрпИропрпЖрой роЕроЯрпИроХрпНроХро▓роорпН роХрпКрогрпНроЯроЮрпНроЪро▓рпН родроирпНродрпБ роОройрпН роЕро┤ро▓ро╛ро░ роиро┐ро┤ро▓ро╛ро░ роЕро│ро┐роХрпНроХро┐ройрпНро▒ро╛ройрпЗ. ennatu yAn ceikinREn ennAtArukku innaDimai tantaLippAn imaiyOr vAzhum
ponnulakil tiruvuDanE amarnta nAthan

187

punalArum  pozhilarangam tikazha mannit

tannakalam akalAta takavAlOngum
takavuDanE tan karumam tAne eNNi annaiyena aDaikkalam koNDu ancal tantu en azhalAra nizhalAra aLikkinRAnE.

Panguni utthiram serti sevai - SrIrangam Meaning:
SrIman nArAyaNa, Who is being rendered break-less service by the nitya sUris, in SrIvaikuNTham, is present in SrIrangam in the reclining posture in

188

order to grace the persons who are not of ego-centric and without the sense of ownership, the benefit of serving Him here itself. The compassion He has by His nature towards the cetana-s, increases more and more due to His association with His Consort, SrI. Such compassionate Lord stands here as my own mother, giving protection to me as though it is His own duty and graces me with the shade of His feet removing all my sufferings in this samsAra world! родрпНро╡ропро╛родро┐роХро╛ро░роорпН роорпБро▒рпНро▒рпБроорпН Thus ends the dvayAdhikAra of SrI sArasAram Srimate nigamAnta mahA deSikAya nama: aDiyEn dAsan Anbil S. SrInivAsan

Note: Chapter 3 of sAra sAram, carama slokAdhikAram to be continued in Volume 3
